public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        int scores[] = new int[]{1, 8, 7, 6, 5, 7, 6, 11, 23};
        int newscores[] = new int[]{5, 7, 8, 7, 9, 4, 5, 6, 9, 8, 7, 4, 5, 1, 2, 3, 5};
        System.out.println("åŸæ•°ç»„çš„å†…å®¹å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š");
        for (int i : scores)
        {
            System.out.print(i + "\t");
        }
        System.out.println();
        System.out.println("ç›®æ ‡æ•°ç»„å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š");
        for (int i : newscores)
        {
            System.out.print(i + "\t");
        }
        System.arraycopy(scores, 0, newscores, 2, 8);
        System.out.println();
        System.out.println("æ›¿æ¢åçš„ç›®æ ‡æ•°ç»„å†…å®¹å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š");
        for (int i : newscores)
        {
            System.out.print(i + "\t");
        }
        System.out.println();
    }
}

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        // å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªaæ•°ç»„
        int[] a = new int[]{3, 4, 5, 6};
        // å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªa2æ•°ç»„
        int[] a2 = new int[]{3, 4, 5, 6};
        // aæ•°ç»„å’Œa2æ•°ç»„çš„é•¿åº¦ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ä¾æ¬¡ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œå°†è¾“å‡ºtrue
        System.out.println("aæ•°ç»„å’Œa2æ•°ç»„æ˜¯å¦ç›¸ç­‰ï¼š" + Arrays.equals(a, a2));
        // é€šè¿‡å¤åˆ¶aæ•°ç»„ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªæ–°çš„bæ•°ç»„
        int[] b = Arrays.copyOf(a, 6);
        System.out.println("aæ•°ç»„å’Œbæ•°ç»„æ˜¯å¦ç›¸ç­‰ï¼š" + Arrays.equals(a, b));
        // è¾“å‡ºbæ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Œå°†è¾“å‡º[3, 4, 5, 6, 0, 0]
        System.out.println("b æ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸ºï¼š" + Arrays.toString(b));
        // å°†bæ•°ç»„çš„ç¬¬3ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ï¼ˆåŒ…æ‹¬ï¼‰åˆ°ç¬¬5ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ï¼ˆä¸åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼‰è³¦å€¼ä¸º1
        Arrays.fill(b, 2, 4, 1);
        // è¾“å‡ºbæ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Œå°†è¾“å‡º[3, 4, 1, 1, 0, 0]
        System.out.println("b æ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸ºï¼š" + Arrays.toString(b));
        // å¯¹bæ•°ç»„è¿›è¡Œæ’åº
        Arrays.sort(b);
        // è¾“å‡ºbæ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ .å°†è¾“å‡º[0,0,1,1,3,4]
        System.out.println("bæ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸ºï¼š" + Arrays.toString(b));
    }
}

public class test2
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        int[] arr1 = new int[]{3, 4, 25, 16, 30, 18};
        // å¯¹æ•°ç»„arr1è¿›è¡Œå¹¶å‘æ’åº
        Arrays.parallelSort(arr1);
        System.out.println(Arrays.toString(arr1));
        int[] arr2 = new int[]{13, -4, 25, 16, 30, 18};
        Arrays.parallelPrefix(arr2, new IntBinaryOperator()
        {
            // left ä»£è¡¨æ•°ç»„ä¸­å‰ä¸€ä¸ªç´¢å¼•å¤„çš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Œè®¡ç®—ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ æ—¶ï¼Œleftä¸º1
            // rightä»£è¡¨æ•°ç»„ä¸­å½“å‰ç´¢å¼•å¤„çš„å…ƒç´ 
            public int applyAsInt(int left, int right)
            {
                return left * right;
            }
        });
        System.out.println(Arrays.toString(arr2));
        int[] arr3 = new int[5];
        Arrays.parallelSetAll(arr3, new IntUnaryOperator()
        {
            // operandä»£è¡¨æ­£åœ¨è®¡ç®—çš„å…ƒç´ ç´¢å¼•
            public int applyAsInt(int operand)
            {
                return operand * 5;
            }
        });
        System.out.println(Arrays.toString(arr3));
    }
}

            System.out.print(i + "\t");

public class test

    {
        int number = 1, result = 1;
        do
        {
            result *= number;
            number++;

        while (number <= 10);

 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šforeachè¯­å¥
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š foreach å¾ªç¯è¯­å¥æ˜¯ Java 1.5 çš„æ–°ç‰¹å¾ä¹‹ä¸€ï¼Œåœ¨éå†æ•°ç»„ã€é›†åˆæ–¹é¢ï¼Œ
 * foreach ä¸ºå¼€å‘è€…æä¾›äº†æå¤§çš„æ–¹ä¾¿ã€‚foreach å¾ªç¯è¯­å¥æ˜¯ for è¯­å¥çš„ç‰¹æ®Šç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆæœ¬ï¼Œä¸»è¦ç”¨äºæ‰§è¡Œéå†åŠŸèƒ½çš„å¾ªç¯ã€‚

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        int[] numbers = {43, 44, 45, 56, 67, 8, 99, 71};
        for (int i = 0; i < numbers.length; i++)
        {
            System.out.println(numbers[i]);
        }
        System.out.println("foreachè¯­å¥ï¼š");
        for (int i : numbers)
        {
            System.out.println(i);
        }
        //item ä¸æ˜¯å¾ªç¯å˜é‡ï¼Œå®ƒä¿å­˜äº†é›†åˆä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Œfor-each è¯­å¥å°†é›†åˆä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸€ä¸€å–å‡ºæ¥ï¼Œ
        // å¹¶ä¿å­˜åˆ° item ä¸­ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªè¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­ä¸éœ€è¦ä½¿ç”¨å¾ªç¯å˜é‡ï¼Œé€šè¿‡æ•°ç»„ä¸‹æ ‡è®¿é—®æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ ã€‚
        // å¯è§ for-each è¯­å¥åœ¨éå†é›†åˆçš„æ—¶å€™è¦ç®€å•æ–¹ä¾¿å¾—å¤šã€‚
        String[] s = {"12345", "hello", "you"};
        for (String si : s)
        {

unsigned __int64 t1, t2, t3, t4;
double run_time;                                                   //å¾®ç§’çº§ç®—æ³•æ—¶é—´è®¡æ—¶å™¨
LARGE_INTEGER time_start;	                                //å¼€å§‹æ—¶é—´
LARGE_INTEGER time_over;	                                //ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
double dqFreq;		                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡
LARGE_INTEGER f;	                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡

inline void runstart()
{
	QueryPerformanceFrequency(&f);
	dqFreq = (double)f.QuadPart;
	t1 = __rdtsc();
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_start);	       //è®¡æ—¶å¼€å§‹
}
inline void runend()
{
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_over);	        //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ
	run_time = 1000 * (time_over.QuadPart - time_start.QuadPart) / dqFreq;
	t2 = __rdtsc();
	t3 = t2 - t1;
}
void ShowProcessMemoryUsageInfo()
{
	HANDLE handle = GetCurrentProcess();
	PROCESS_MEMORY_COUNTERS pmc;
	GetProcessMemoryInfo(handle, &pmc, sizeof(pmc));
	float memoryUsage_M = pmc.WorkingSetSize / (1024.0 * 1024.0);
	float memoryUsage_K = pmc.WorkingSetSize / 1024.0;
	std::cout << std::fixed << setprecision(0) << "ç¨‹åºå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << memoryUsage_K << " KB = " << setprecision(2) << memoryUsage_M << " MB" << std::endl;
}
__int64 CompareFileTime(FILETIME time1, FILETIME time2)//è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•´æ•°æ—¶é—´
{
	__int64 a = static_cast<long long>(time1.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time1.dwLowDateTime;
	__int64 b = static_cast<long long>(time2.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time2.dwLowDateTime;
	return   (b - a);
}

//**************************************************************//************************éä¸»å‡½æ•°

// æå–æŒ‡å®šæ¨¡å—ä¸­çš„èµ„æºæ–‡ä»¶
// å‚æ•°ï¼š
//     strDstFile:     ç›®æ ‡æ–‡ä»¶åã€‚æå–çš„èµ„æºå°†ä¿å­˜åœ¨è¿™é‡Œï¼›
//     strResType:     èµ„æºç±»å‹ï¼›
//     strResName:     èµ„æºåç§°ï¼›
// è¿”å›å€¼ï¼š
//     true: æ‰§è¡ŒæˆåŠŸï¼›
//     false: æ‰§è¡Œå¤±è´¥ã€‚

bool ExtractResource(LPCTSTR strDstFile, LPCTSTR strResType, LPCTSTR strResName)
{
	// åˆ›å»ºæ–‡ä»¶
	HANDLE hFile = ::CreateFile(strDstFile, GENERIC_WRITE, NULL, NULL, CREATE_ALWAYS, FILE_ATTRIBUTE_TEMPORARY, NULL);
	if (hFile == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE)
		return false;

	// æŸ¥æ‰¾èµ„æºæ–‡ä»¶ä¸­ã€åŠ è½½èµ„æºåˆ°å†…å­˜ã€å¾—åˆ°èµ„æºå¤§å°
	HRSRC    hRes = ::FindResource(NULL, strResName, strResType);
	HGLOBAL    hMem = ::LoadResource(NULL, hRes);
	DWORD    dwSize = ::SizeofResource(NULL, hRes);

	// å†™å…¥æ–‡ä»¶
	DWORD dwWrite = 0; // è¿”å›å†™å…¥å­—èŠ‚
	::WriteFile(hFile, hMem, dwSize, &dwWrite, NULL);
	::CloseHandle(hFile);

	return true;
}

char* Wchar2char(const wchar_t* szStr)
{
	int nLen = WideCharToMultiByte(CP_ACP, 0, szStr, -1, NULL, 0, NULL, NULL);
	if (nLen == 0)
	{
		return NULL;
	}
	char* pResult = new char[nLen];
	WideCharToMultiByte(CP_ACP, 0, szStr, -1, pResult, nLen, NULL, NULL);
	return pResult;
}

string GetExePath()
{
	char szFilePath[MAX_PATH + 1] = { 0 };
	GetModuleFileNameA(NULL, szFilePath, MAX_PATH);
	/*
	strrchr:å‡½æ•°åŠŸèƒ½ï¼šæŸ¥æ‰¾ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦cåœ¨å¦ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²strä¸­æœ«æ¬¡å‡ºç°çš„ä½ç½®ï¼ˆä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯ä»strçš„å³ä¾§å¼€å§‹æŸ¥æ‰¾å­—ç¬¦cé¦–æ¬¡å‡ºç°çš„ä½ç½®ï¼‰ï¼Œ
	å¹¶è¿”å›è¿™ä¸ªä½ç½®çš„åœ°å€ã€‚å¦‚æœæœªèƒ½æ‰¾åˆ°æŒ‡å®šå­—ç¬¦ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå‡½æ•°å°†è¿”å›NULLã€‚
	ä½¿ç”¨è¿™ä¸ªåœ°å€è¿”å›ä»æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦cåˆ°stræœ«å°¾çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚
	*/
	(strrchr(szFilePath, '\\'))[0] = 0; // åˆ é™¤æ–‡ä»¶åï¼Œåªè·å¾—è·¯å¾„å­—ä¸²//
	string path = szFilePath;
	return path;
}

void getFiles(string path, vector<string>& files)
{
	//æ–‡ä»¶å¥æŸ„
	long   hFile = 0;
	//æ–‡ä»¶ä¿¡æ¯
	struct _finddata_t fileinfo;
	string p;
	if ((hFile = _findfirst(p.assign(path).append("\\*").c_str(), &fileinfo)) != -1)
	{
		do
		{
			//å¦‚æœæ˜¯ç›®å½•,è¿­ä»£ä¹‹
			//å¦‚æœä¸æ˜¯,åŠ å…¥åˆ—è¡¨
			if ((fileinfo.attrib & _A_SUBDIR))
			{
				if (strcmp(fileinfo.name, ".") != 0 && strcmp(fileinfo.name, "..") != 0)
					getFiles(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name), files);
			}
			else
			{
				files.push_back(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name));
			}
		} while (_findnext(hFile, &fileinfo) == 0);
		_findclose(hFile);
	}
}

void getFilesAll(string path, vector<string>& files)
{
	//æ–‡ä»¶å¥æŸ„
	long hFile = 0;
	//æ–‡ä»¶ä¿¡æ¯
	struct _finddata_t fileinfo;
	string p;
	if ((hFile = _findfirst(p.assign(path).append("\\*").c_str(), &fileinfo)) != -1)
	{
		do
		{
			if ((fileinfo.attrib & _A_SUBDIR))
			{
				if (strcmp(fileinfo.name, ".") != 0 && strcmp(fileinfo.name, "..") != 0)
				{
					//files.push_back(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name));
					getFilesAll(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name), files);
				}
			}
			else
			{
				files.push_back(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name));
			}
		} while (_findnext(hFile, &fileinfo) == 0);
		_findclose(hFile);
	}
}

string solve(string& s1, string& s2)
{
	if (s2.size() == 0)
		return s1;
	for (int i = 0;i < (int)(s1.size() - s2.size() + 1);)
	{
		if (s1.substr(i, s2.size()) == s2)
		{
			s1.erase(i, s2.size());
		}
		else
			i++;
	}
	return s1;
}

/*
path: æŒ‡å®šç›®å½•
files: ä¿å­˜ç»“æœ
fileType: æŒ‡å®šçš„æ–‡ä»¶æ ¼å¼ï¼Œå¦‚ .jpg
*/
void getAllFiles(string path, vector<string>& files, string fileType)
{
	// æ–‡ä»¶å¥æŸ„
	long hFile = 0;
	// æ–‡ä»¶ä¿¡æ¯
	struct _finddata_t fileinfo;

	string p;

	if ((hFile = _findfirst(p.assign(path).append("\\*" + fileType).c_str(), &fileinfo)) != -1) {
		do {
			// ä¿å­˜æ–‡ä»¶çš„å…¨è·¯å¾„
			files.push_back(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name));

		} while (_findnext(hFile, &fileinfo) == 0); //å¯»æ‰¾ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªï¼ŒæˆåŠŸè¿”å›0ï¼Œå¦åˆ™-1

		_findclose(hFile);
	}
}

BOOL SetConsoleColor(WORD wAttributes)
{
	HANDLE hConsole = GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE);
	if (hConsole == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE)
		return FALSE;
	return SetConsoleTextAttribute(hConsole, wAttributes);
}

#define FOREGROUND_GREEN     0x0002 // text color contains green.
#define FOREGROUND_RED       0x0004 // text color contains red.
#define FOREGROUND_INTENSITY 0x0008 // text color is intensified.æ–‡æœ¬é¢œè‰²å¢å¼ºã€‚
#define BACKGROUND_BLUE      0x0010 // background color contains blue.//èƒŒæ™¯è‰²åŒ…å«è“è‰²ã€‚
#define BACKGROUND_GREEN     0x0020 // background color contains green.
#define BACKGROUND_RED       0x0040 // background color contains red.
#define BACKGROUND_INTENSITY 0x0080 // background color is intensified.
#define COMMON_LVB_LEADING_BYTE    0x0100 // Leading Byte of DBCS
#define COMMON_LVB_TRAILING_BYTE   0x0200 // Trailing Byte of DBCS
#define COMMON_LVB_GRID_HORIZONTAL 0x0400 // DBCS: Grid attribute: top horizontal.
#define COMMON_LVB_GRID_LVERTICAL  0x0800 // DBCS: Grid attribute: left vertical.
#define COMMON_LVB_GRID_RVERTICAL  0x1000 // DBCS: Grid attribute: right vertical.

#define COMMON_LVB_UNDERSCORE      0x8000 // DBCS: Underscore.
#define COMMON_LVB_SBCSDBCS        0x0300 // SBCS or DBCS flag.

import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šJava if elseåˆ†æ”¯ç»“æ„
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š ç¼–å†™ä¸€ä¸ª Java ç¨‹åºï¼Œå…è®¸ç”¨æˆ·ä»é”®ç›˜è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—ï¼Œå†åˆ¤æ–­è¯¥æ•°æ˜¯å¦å¤§äº 100

 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/9/20
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 20:43
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—ï¼š");
        Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
        int num;
        num = input.nextInt();
        if (num > 100)
        {
            System.out.println("è¾“å…¥çš„æ•°å­—å¤§äº100");
        }
        else if (num == 100)
        {
            System.out.println("è¾“å…¥çš„æ•°å­—ç­‰äº100");
        }
        else
        {
            System.out.println("è¾“å…¥çš„æ•°å­—å°äº100");
        }
    }

import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šjavaé¡¹ç›®å®æˆ˜   æ ¹æ®å‡ºç”Ÿæ—¥æœŸè®¡ç®—ï¼ˆåˆ¤æ–­ï¼‰æ˜Ÿåº§

 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 20:44
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0

public class Switch
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥æ‚¨çš„å‡ºç”Ÿå¹´æœˆï¼ˆå¦‚ 0123 è¡¨ç¤º 1 æœˆ 23 æ—¥ï¼‰ï¼š");
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        int month_day = sc.nextInt();
        int month = month_day / 100;
        int day = month_day % 100;
        String constellation = "";
        switch (month)
        {
            case 1:
                constellation = day < 21 ? "æ‘©ç¾¯åº§" : "æ°´ç“¶åº§";
                break;
            case 2:
                constellation = day < 20 ? "æ°´ç“¶åº§" : "åŒé±¼åº§";
                break;
            case 3:
                constellation = day < 21 ? "åŒé±¼åº§" : "ç™½ç¾Šåº§";
                break;
            case 4:
                constellation = day < 21 ? "ç™½ç¾Šåº§" : "é‡‘ç‰›åº§";
                break;
            case 5:
                constellation = day < 22 ? "é‡‘ç‰›åº§" : "åŒå­åº§";
                break;
            case 6:
                constellation = day < 22 ? "åŒå­åº§" : "å·¨èŸ¹åº§";
                break;
            case 7:
                constellation = day < 23 ? "å·¨èŸ¹åº§" : "ç‹®å­åº§";
                break;
            case 8:
                constellation = day < 24 ? "ç‹®å­åº§" : "å¤„å¥³åº§";
                break;
            case 9:
                constellation = day < 24 ? "å¤„å¥³åº§" : "å¤©ç§¤åº§";
                break;
            case 10:
                constellation = day < 24 ? "å¤©ç§¤åº§" : "å¤©èåº§";
                break;
            case 11:
                constellation = day < 23 ? "å¤©èåº§" : "å°„æ‰‹åº§";
                break;
            case 12:
                constellation = day < 22 ? "å°„æ‰‹åº§" : "æ‘©ç¾¯åº§";
                break;
        }
        System.out.println("æ‚¨çš„æ˜Ÿåº§æ˜¯ï¼š" + constellation);
    }

unsigned __int64 t1, t2, t3, t4;
double run_time;                                                   //å¾®ç§’çº§ç®—æ³•æ—¶é—´è®¡æ—¶å™¨
LARGE_INTEGER time_start;	                                //å¼€å§‹æ—¶é—´
LARGE_INTEGER time_over;	                                //ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
double dqFreq;		                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡
LARGE_INTEGER f;	                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡

inline void runstart()
{
	QueryPerformanceFrequency(&f);
	dqFreq = (double)f.QuadPart;
	t1 = __rdtsc();
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_start);	       //è®¡æ—¶å¼€å§‹
}
inline void runend()
{
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_over);	        //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ
	run_time = 1000 * (time_over.QuadPart - time_start.QuadPart) / dqFreq;
	t2 = __rdtsc();
	t3 = t2 - t1;
}
void ShowProcessMemoryUsageInfo()
{
	HANDLE handle = GetCurrentProcess();
	PROCESS_MEMORY_COUNTERS pmc;
	GetProcessMemoryInfo(handle, &pmc, sizeof(pmc));
	float memoryUsage_M = pmc.WorkingSetSize / (1024.0 * 1024.0);
	float memoryUsage_K = pmc.WorkingSetSize / 1024.0;
	std::cout << std::fixed << setprecision(0) << "ç¨‹åºå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << memoryUsage_K << " KB = " << setprecision(2) << memoryUsage_M << " MB" << std::endl;
}
__int64 CompareFileTime(FILETIME time1, FILETIME time2)//è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•´æ•°æ—¶é—´
{
	__int64 a = static_cast<long long>(time1.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time1.dwLowDateTime;
	__int64 b = static_cast<long long>(time2.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time2.dwLowDateTime;
	return   (b - a);
}

		cursorPos.X = 0;

		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "æŒ‰ä»»æ„é”®é€€å‡ºç¨‹åº" << endl;
		preidleTime = idleTime;
		prekernelTime = kernelTime;
		preuserTime = userTime;
	}
	cout << endl;
	
}


//**************************************************************//************************éä¸»å‡½æ•°

#include <shobjidl.h>  
#include <shlguid.h>  
#include <locale.h>  

#include<shlwapi.h>

static HRESULT ResolveIt(HWND hwnd, TCHAR* lpszLinkFile, TCHAR* lpszPath, int iPathBufferSize)
{
	HRESULT hres;
	IShellLink* psl;
	WIN32_FIND_DATA wfd;
	*lpszPath = 0; // Assume failure   
	// Get a pointer to the IShellLink interface. It is assumed that CoInitialize  
	// has already been called.   
	hres = CoCreateInstance(CLSID_ShellLink, NULL, CLSCTX_INPROC_SERVER, IID_IShellLink, (LPVOID*)&psl);
	if (SUCCEEDED(hres))
	{
		IPersistFile* ppf;
		// Get a pointer to the IPersistFile interface.   
		hres = psl->QueryInterface(IID_IPersistFile, (void**)&ppf);
		if (SUCCEEDED(hres))
		{
			// Add code here to check return value from MultiByteWideChar   
			// for success.  

			// Load the shortcut.   
			hres = ppf->Load(lpszLinkFile, STGM_READ);

			if (SUCCEEDED(hres))
			{
				// Resolve the link.   
				hres = psl->Resolve(hwnd, 0);
				if (SUCCEEDED(hres))
				{
					// Get the path to the link target.   
					hres = psl->GetPath(lpszPath, MAX_PATH, (WIN32_FIND_DATA*)&wfd, SLGP_RAWPATH/*SLGP_SHORTPATH*/);
				}
			}
			// Release the pointer to the IPersistFile interface.   
			ppf->Release();
		}
		// Release the pointer to the IShellLink interface.   
		psl->Release();
	}
	return hres;
}

BOOL SetConsoleColor(WORD wAttributes)
{
	HANDLE hConsole = GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE);
	if (hConsole == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE)
		return FALSE;
	return SetConsoleTextAttribute(hConsole, wAttributes);
}

{

	//*************************************************************************



	//*************************************************************************
	runstart();
	//*************************è®¡æ—¶å¼€å§‹***************************************
	
	SetConsoleColor(FOREGROUND_GREEN | FOREGROUND_INTENSITY);    //ç»¿

	CoInitialize(NULL);
	ResolveIt(NULL, szLinkFilePath, szLinkFileExePath, MAX_PATH);
	wprintf(L"%s\n", szLinkFileExePath);
	CoUninitialize();
	PathStripPath(szLinkFileExePath);                //æ ¹æ®è·¯å¾„åè¾“å‡ºæ–‡ä»¶å
	wprintf(L"%s\n", szLinkFileExePath);            
	SetConsoleColor(FOREGROUND_RED | FOREGROUND_GREEN | FOREGROUND_BLUE);

	//*************************è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ***************************************
	runend();



	



	rundisplay();                                                                   //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æœæ˜¾ç¤º

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šnçš‡åé—®é¢˜
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/9/17
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 19:24
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 */

public class Queen
{
    private int n;
    private long count;
    private int[] arr;
//    private int nn;

    public Queen(int n)
    {
        this.n = n;
        //      nn = (1 << n) - 1;
        count = 0;
        arr = new int[n];
    }

    public boolean Check(int row, int col)
    {
        for (int i = 0; i < row; i++)
        {
            if (col == arr[i] || Math.abs(row - i) == Math.abs(col - arr[i])) //åœ¨åŒä¸€åˆ—æˆ–è€…åœ¨åŒä¸€æ–œçº¿ã€‚ä¸€å®šä¸åœ¨åŒä¸€è¡Œ
            {
                return false;
            }
        }
        return true;
    }

    public void FindNQueen(int k)
    {
        if (k == n)
        {   //æ±‚å‡ºä¸€ç§è§£ï¼Œ count+1
            count++;
            return;
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        {
            if (Check(k, i))
            {   //æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦æ»¡è¶³æ¡ä»¶
                arr[k] = i;      //è®°å½•
                FindNQueen(k + 1);   //é€’å½’æŸ¥æ‰¾
            }
        }
    }

    public static void main(String args[])
    {
        Queen nQueen = new Queen(13);
        nQueen.FindNQueen(0);
        System.out.println("æ€»æ•°ï¼š"+nQueen.count);
    }

}

class MyComparator implements Comparator<Integer>
{
    @Override
    public int compare(Integer o1, Integer o2)
    {
        /*
         * å¦‚æœo1å°äºo2ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°±è¿”å›æ­£å€¼ï¼Œå¦‚æœo1å¤§äºo2æˆ‘ä»¬å°±è¿”å›è´Ÿå€¼ï¼Œ è¿™æ ·é¢ å€’ä¸€ä¸‹ï¼Œå°±å¯ä»¥å®ç°é™åºæ’åºäº†,åä¹‹å³å¯è‡ªå®šä¹‰å‡åºæ’åºäº†
         */
        return o2 - o1;
    }
}

{

    {

        System.out.println("åœ¨é™æ€æ–¹æ³• method2()ä¸­çš„ count=" + count);    // æ‰“å°count

    }

        // é€šè¿‡ç±»åè°ƒç”¨é™æ€æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ‰“å° count
        test2.PrintCount();

        {
             double final_runtime;

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šStringBufferæ›¿æ¢ç‰¹æ®Šå­—ç¬¦  replace-special-characters
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/10/2
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 19:58
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š åœ¨æœ¬å®ä¾‹ä¸­ä¸ºä¿è¯å­¦ç”Ÿè¾“å…¥çš„ Java æ–‡ä»¶ååˆæ ¼ï¼Œå°†åˆ©ç”¨ StringBuffer ç±»å®ç°å¯¹ Java æ–‡ä»¶åä¸­çš„ç‰¹æ®Šç¬¦å·è¿›è¡Œæ›¿æ¢ï¼Œ
 * åŒ…æ‹¬å°†ä¸­æ–‡çŠ¶æ€ä¸‹çš„â€œã€‚â€å’Œå…¨è§’çŠ¶æ€ä¸‹çš„â€œ.â€æ›¿æ¢ä¸ºè‹±æ–‡çŠ¶æ€ä¸‹çš„â€œ.â€ã€‚
 */

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥æ–‡ä»¶åï¼š");
        String filename = input.next();

        long startTime = System.nanoTime();   //è·å–å¼€å§‹æ—¶é—´
        //------------------------------------------------------



        StringBuffer file = new StringBuffer(filename);
        // è·å–è‹±æ–‡çŠ¶æ€ä¸‹çš„"."æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨
        int index = file.lastIndexOf(".");
        // åˆ¤æ–­ä¸­æ–‡çŠ¶æ€ä¸‹çš„"ã€‚"å’Œ"."æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨
        int errIndex1 = file.lastIndexOf("ã€‚");
        int errIndex2 = file.lastIndexOf(".");
        if (index != -1 && file.substring(index + 1, file.length()).equals("java"))
        {
            System.out.println("ä½œä¸šæäº¤æˆåŠŸ!");
        }
        else if (errIndex1 != -1 && file.substring(errIndex1 + 1, file.length()).equals("java"))
        {
            file.setCharAt(errIndex1, '.');
            System.out.println("ä½ çš„ä¹¦å†™æœ‰è¯¯ï¼Œå·²æ”¹æ­£ä¸ºï¼š" + file + "\r\næäº¤æˆåŠŸï¼");
        }
        else if (errIndex2 != -1 && file.substring(errIndex2 + 1, file.length()).equals("java"))
        {
            // å°†å…¨è§’çŠ¶æ€ä¸‹çš„"."æ”¹ä¸ºè‹±æ–‡çŠ¶æ€ä¸‹çš„"."
            file.setCharAt(errIndex2, '.');
            System.out.println("ä½ çš„ä¹¦å†™æœ‰è¯¯ï¼Œå·²æ”¹æ­£ä¸ºï¼š" + file + "\r\næäº¤æˆåŠŸï¼");
        }
        else
        {
            System.out.println("ä½ æä¾›çš„javaæ–‡ä»¶åç§°æœ‰è¯¯ï¼Œè¯·æ ¸å®ï¼");
        }


        //------------------------------------------------------
        long endTime = System.nanoTime(); //è·å–ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
        if ((endTime - startTime) < 1000000)
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime);
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "å¾®ç§’");
        }
        else if ((endTime - startTime) >= 1000000 && (endTime - startTime) < 10000000000L)
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 1000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "æ¯«ç§’");
        }
        else
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 10000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 100000;

            double final_runtime;

            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;

{
    protected String name;
    protected int age;
    protected String sex;
    protected int id = 12345;

    {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.sex = sex;
    }

    public People(String name, int age)
    {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    void message()
    {
        System.out.println("This is person class");
    }
}

        //------------------------------------------------------

        s.display();
        Cat cat = new Cat("åŠ¨ç‰©", "çŒ«");
        cat.display();
        System.out.println();
        //------------------------------------------------------
        long endTime = System.nanoTime(); //è·å–ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
        if ((endTime - startTime) < 1000000)
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime);
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "å¾®ç§’");
        }
        else if ((endTime - startTime) >= 1000000 && (endTime - startTime) < 10000000000L)
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 1000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "æ¯«ç§’");
        }
        else
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 10000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 100000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "ç§’");
        }
        Runtime r = Runtime.getRuntime();
        float memory;
        memory = r.totalMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf("JVMæ€»å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);
        memory = r.freeMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf(" ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);
        memory = r.totalMemory() - r.freeMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf("å·²ä½¿ç”¨çš„å†…å­˜ï¼š%.4fMB\n", memory);
        //------------------------------------------------------
    }
}

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        int x, y, z; // å£°æ˜ä¸‰ä¸ªå˜é‡
        System.out.print("è¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ï¼š");
        Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
        x = input.nextInt(); // ç”±ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥xçš„å€¼
        // åˆ¤æ–­xçš„å€¼æ˜¯å¦å¤§äº5ï¼Œå¦‚æœæ˜¯y=xï¼Œå¦åˆ™y=-x
        y = x > 5 ? x : -x;
        // åˆ¤æ–­yçš„å€¼æ˜¯å¦å¤§äºxï¼Œå¦‚æœæ˜¯z=yï¼Œå¦åˆ™z=5
        z = y > x ? y : 5;
        System.out.printf("x=%d \n", x);
        System.out.printf("y=%d \n", y);
        System.out.printf("z=%d \n", z);
    }

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šä¸è§„åˆ™æ•°ç»„
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/9/24
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 16:59
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 */

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        int[][] array = new int[4][];
        array[0] = new int[3];
        array[1] = new int[1];
        array[2] = new int[2];
        array[3] = new int[4];
        for (int i = 0; i < array.length; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < array[i].length; j++)
            {
                array[i][j] = i + j;
            }
        }
        for (int[] row : array)
        {
            for (int i : row)
            {
                System.out.printf("%d\t", i);
            }
            System.out.println();
        }
    }
}

 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šäºŒç»´æ•°ç»„  è·å–è¡Œå’Œåˆ—çš„æ‰€æœ‰æ•°æ®

public class test_i
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        double[][] class_score = {{100, 99, 99}, {100, 98, 97}, {100, 100, 99.5}, {99.5, 99, 98.5}};
        Scanner scan = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.println("å½“å‰æ•°ç»„åªæœ‰" + class_score.length + "è¡Œï¼Œæ‚¨æƒ³æŸ¥çœ‹ç¬¬å‡ è¡Œçš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Ÿè¯·è¾“å…¥ï¼š");
        int number;
        while (true)
        {
            number = scan.nextInt();
            if (number <= class_score.length)
            {
                break;
            }
            else
            {
                System.out.println("è¾“å…¥é”™è¯¯ï¼Œè¯·é‡æ–°è¾“å…¥ï¼");
            }
        }
        for (int j = 0; j < class_score[number - 1].length; j++)
        {
            System.out.println("ç¬¬" + number + "è¡Œçš„ç¬¬[" + j + "]ä¸ªå…ƒç´ çš„å€¼æ˜¯ï¼š" + class_score[number - 1][j]);
        }
    }

        System.out.println("æ‚¨è¦è·å–å“ªä¸€åˆ—çš„å€¼ï¼Ÿè¯·è¾“å…¥ï¼š");

        while (true)
        {
            number = scan.nextInt();
            if (number <= class_score[0].length)
            {
                break;
            }
            else
            {
                System.out.println("è¾“å…¥é”™è¯¯ï¼Œè¯·é‡æ–°è¾“å…¥ï¼");
            }
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < class_score.length; i++)
        {
            System.out.println("ç¬¬ " + (i + 1) + " è¡Œçš„ç¬¬[" + number + "]ä¸ªå…ƒç´ çš„å€¼æ˜¯" + class_score[i][number - 1]);

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šäºŒç»´æ•°ç»„  éšæœºæ•°
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š å‡è®¾æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªçŸ©é˜µä¸º 5 è¡Œ 5 åˆ—ï¼Œè¯¥çŸ©é˜µæ˜¯ç”±ç¨‹åºéšæœºäº§ç”Ÿçš„ 10 ä»¥å†…æ•°å­—æ’åˆ—è€Œæˆã€‚ä¸‹é¢ä½¿ç”¨äºŒç»´æ•°ç»„æ¥åˆ›å»ºè¯¥çŸ©é˜µï¼Œä»£ç å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/9/23
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 20:12
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        double[][] data = new double[10][10];
        for (int i = 0; i < data.length; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < data[i].length; j++)
            {
                data[i][j] = (double) (Math.random() * 10000);
            }
        }
        System.out.println("ä¸‹é¢æ˜¯ç¨‹åºç”Ÿæˆçš„çŸ©é˜µ\n");
        // éå†äºŒç»´çŸ©é˜µå¹¶è¾“å‡º
        double max = 0;
        double min = 999999999999.0;
        double total = 0;
        int num = data.length * data[0].length;
        for (int k = 0; k < data.length; k++)
        {
            for (int g = 0; g < data[k].length; g++)
            {
                System.out.printf("%.2f\t\t", data[k][g]);
                if (max < data[k][g])
                {
                    max = data[k][g];
                }
                if (min > data[k][g])
                {
                    min = data[k][g];
                }
                total = total + data[k][g];
            }
            System.out.println();
        }
        System.out.printf("æœ€å¤§å€¼ï¼š%.2f\t\t", max);
        System.out.printf("æœ€å°å€¼ï¼š%.2f\t\t", min);
        System.out.printf("å¹³å‡å€¼ï¼š%.2f\n", total / num);
    }
}

import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šäº”å­æ£‹æ¸¸æˆ gobang_game
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/9/27
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 20:34
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 */

public class Gobang
{
    // å®šä¹‰æ£‹ç›˜çš„å¤§å°
    public static int BOARD_SIZE = 15;
    // å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªäºŒç»´æ•°ç»„æ¥å……å½“æ£‹ç›˜
    public static String[][] board = new String[BOARD_SIZE][BOARD_SIZE];
    String black = "â—"; // é»‘å­
    String white = "â—‹"; // ç™½å­

    /**
     * åˆå§‹åŒ–æ¢°ç›˜æ•°ç»„
     */
    public void initBoard()
    {
        // æŠŠæ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ èµ‹ä¸º"â•‹"ï¼Œç”¨äºåœ¨æ§åˆ¶å°ç”»å‡ºæ£‹ç›˜
        for (int i = 0; i < BOARD_SIZE; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < BOARD_SIZE; j++)
            {
                board[i][j] = "â•‹";
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * åœ¨æ§åˆ¶å°è¾“å‡ºæ£‹ç›˜çš„æ–¹æ³•
     */
    public void printBoard()
    {
        // æ‰“å°æ¯ä¸ªæ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ 
        for (int i = 0; i < BOARD_SIZE; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < BOARD_SIZE; j++)
            {
                // æ‰“å°æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ åä¸æ¢è¡Œ
                System.out.print(board[i][j]);
            }
            // æ¯æ‰“å°å®Œä¸€è¡Œæ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ åè¾“å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªæ¢è¡Œç¬¦
            System.out.print("\n");
        }
    }

    /**
     * åˆ¤æ–­è¾“èµ¢çš„æ–¹æ³•
     */
    public static boolean isWin(int x, int y, String color)
    {
        if (color.equals("black"))
        {
            color = "â—";
        }
        if (color.equals("white"))
        {
            color = "â—‹";
        }
        // æ¨ªå‘
        for (int i = 0; i < board.length - 5; i++)
        {
            if (board[x][i].equals(color) && board[x][i + 1].equals(color) && board[x][i + 2].equals(color)
                    && board[x][i + 3].equals(color) && board[x][i + 4].equals(color))
            {
                return true;
            }
        }
        // ç«–å‘
        for (int i = 0; i < board.length - 5; i++)
        {
            if (board[i][y].equals(color) && board[i + 1][y].equals(color) && board[i + 2][y].equals(color)
                    && board[i + 3][y].equals(color) && board[i + 4][y].equals(color))
            {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    /**
     * åˆ¤æ–­æŒ‡å®šåæ ‡æ˜¯å¦æœ‰æ£‹å­
     */
    public static boolean isOk(int x, int y)
    {
        if (!board[x - 1][y - 1].equals("â•‹"))
        {
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }

    /**
     * ç”µè„‘ä¸‹æ£‹
     */
    public static String computer(String color)
    {
        int x = (int) (Math.random() * 14) + 1; // ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ª1~14ä¹‹é—´çš„éšæœºæ•°
        int y = (int) (Math.random() * 14) + 1; // ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ª1~14ä¹‹é—´çš„éšæœºæ•°
        // åˆ¤æ–­ç”µè„‘ä¸‹æ£‹çš„åæ ‡æœ‰æ— æ£‹å­ï¼Œæœ‰æ£‹å­åˆ™åœ¨é‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆéšæœºæ•°
        if (isOk(x, y))
        {
            if (color.equals("black"))
            {
                board[x][y] = "â—";
            }
            else if (color.equals("white"))
            {
                board[x][y] = "â—‹";
            }
        }
        else
        {
            computer(color);
        }
        return "x,y";
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception
    {
        Gobang gb = new Gobang();
        gb.initBoard();
        gb.printBoard();
        // è¿™æ˜¯ç”¨äºè·å–é”®ç›˜è¾“å…¥çš„æ–¹æ³•
        Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in); // ä½¿ç”¨Scannerç±»è·å–ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥
        System.out.println("æ‚¨æƒ³è¦é€‰æ‹©ä»€ä¹ˆé¢œè‰²çš„æ£‹ï¼Œblackæˆ–whiteï¼Œè¯·è¾“å…¥ï¼š");
        String peopleColor = input.next(); // å®šä¹‰ç”¨æˆ·é€‰æ‹©æ£‹å­çš„é¢œè‰²å¹¶è¿”å›ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        // å¦‚æœç”¨æˆ·é€‰æ‹©çš„æ˜¯ç™½æ£‹ï¼Œåˆ™ç”µè„‘å…ˆä¸‹ï¼ˆäº”å­æ£‹ä¸­é»‘æ£‹å…ˆä¸‹ï¼‰
        if (peopleColor.equals("white"))
        {
            System.out.println("æ‚¨é€‰æ‹©çš„æ˜¯ç™½æ£‹");
            computer("black");
            gb.printBoard();
        }
        String inputStr;
        do
        {
            System.out.println("è¾“å…¥æ‚¨ä¸‹æ£‹çš„åæ ‡ï¼Œåº”ä»¥x,yçš„æ ¼å¼ï¼š");
            inputStr = input.next();
            // å®šä¹‰æ•°ç»„å¹¶èµ‹å€¼åæ ‡xï¼Œ,y
            String[] posStrArr = inputStr.split(",");
            int x = Integer.parseInt(posStrArr[0]);
            int y = Integer.parseInt(posStrArr[1]);
            // å¦‚æœè¾“å…¥åæ ‡å·²æœ‰æ£‹å­ï¼Œåˆ™é‡æ–°è¾“å…¥åæ ‡
            if (!isOk(x, y))
            {
                System.out.println("æ­¤å¤„å·²æœ‰æ£‹å­ï¼Œè¯·æ¢ä½ç½®ï¼");
                continue;
            }
            // å°†ä¸Šé¢åˆ†éš”å®Œä»¥åçš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²è½¬æ¢æˆç”¨æˆ·ä¸‹æ£‹çš„åæ ‡
            int xPos = x;
            int yPos = y;
            // å®šä¹‰ç”µè„‘æ£‹å­é¢œè‰²
            String comColor = null;
            // æ ¹æ®ç”¨æˆ·é€‰æ‹©çš„æ£‹å­é¢œè‰²ç»™å¯¹åº”çš„æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ èµ‹å€¼
            if (peopleColor.equals("black"))
            {
                gb.board[xPos - 1][yPos - 1] = "â—";
                comColor = "white";
            }
            else if (peopleColor.equals("white"))
            {
                gb.board[xPos - 1][yPos - 1] = "â—‹";
                comColor = "black";
            }
            computer(comColor);
            gb.printBoard();
            // åˆ¤æ–­è¾“èµ¢
            if (isWin(xPos - 1, yPos - 1, peopleColor))
            {
                System.out.println(peopleColor + "è·èƒœï¼");
                break;
            }
            if (isWin(xPos - 1, yPos - 1, comColor))
            {
                System.out.println(comColor + "è·èƒœï¼");
                break;
            }
        }
        while (inputStr != null);
    }
}

using namespace std;

#pragma intrinsic(__rdtsc)
unsigned __int64 t1, t2, t3, t4;
double run_time;                                                   //å¾®ç§’çº§ç®—æ³•æ—¶é—´è®¡æ—¶å™¨
LARGE_INTEGER time_start;	                                //å¼€å§‹æ—¶é—´
LARGE_INTEGER time_over;	                                //ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
double dqFreq;		                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡
LARGE_INTEGER f;	                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡
double tt;
long double totaltime;

inline void runstart()
{
	QueryPerformanceFrequency(&f);
	dqFreq = (double)f.QuadPart;
	t1 = __rdtsc();
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_start);	       //è®¡æ—¶å¼€å§‹
}
inline void runend()
{
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_over);	        //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ
	run_time = 1000 * (time_over.QuadPart - time_start.QuadPart) / dqFreq;
	t2 = __rdtsc();
	t3 = t2 - t1;
}
void ShowProcessMemoryUsageInfo()
{
	HANDLE handle = GetCurrentProcess();
	PROCESS_MEMORY_COUNTERS pmc;
	GetProcessMemoryInfo(handle, &pmc, sizeof(pmc));
	float memoryUsage_M = pmc.WorkingSetSize / (1024.0 * 1024.0);
	float memoryUsage_K = pmc.WorkingSetSize / 1024.0;
	std::cout << std::fixed << setprecision(0) << "ç¨‹åºå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << memoryUsage_K << " KB = " << setprecision(2) << memoryUsage_M << " MB" << std::endl;
}
__int64 CompareFileTime(FILETIME time1, FILETIME time2)//è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•´æ•°æ—¶é—´
{
	__int64 a = static_cast<long long>(time1.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time1.dwLowDateTime;
	__int64 b = static_cast<long long>(time2.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time2.dwLowDateTime;
	return   (b - a);
}

	cout << "æ€»ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << freetotal << " GB" << endl;
	double freevir = (totalvir - freetotal) - (totalphy * statex.dwMemoryLoad / 100.0);
	cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨é‡ï¼š" << setprecision(3) << freevir << " GB" << endl;
	double usevir = freevir * 100 / (totalvir - totalphy);
	cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š";
	printf("%.2f%%", usevir);
	cout << endl;
	cout << "CPUåˆ©ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << right << setprecision(2) << setw(6) << 0.00 << "%" << endl;
	cout << "CPUç©ºé—²ç‡ï¼š    " << setw(6) << 100.0<< "%" << endl;
	cout << "-------------------------------------------------------" << endl;
	cout << "æŒ‰ä»»æ„é”®é€€å‡ºç¨‹åº" << endl;
	while (!_kbhit())
	{
		GlobalMemoryStatusEx(&statex);
		WaitForSingleObject(hEvent, 1000);
		res = GetSystemTimes(&idleTime, &kernelTime, &userTime);
		int idle = CompareFileTime(preidleTime, idleTime);
		int kernel = CompareFileTime(prekernelTime, kernelTime);
		int user = CompareFileTime(preuserTime, userTime);
		float cpu = (kernel + user - idle) * 100.0 / (kernel + user);
		float cpuidle = (idle) * 100.0 / (kernel + user);
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 0;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		//cout << "å†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << statex.dwMemoryLoad << "%" << endl;
		double freephy = statex.ullAvailPhys / 1024 / 1024;
		freephy = freephy / 1024;
		double usephy = (totalphy - freephy) * 100.0 / totalphy;
		cout << "å†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << usephy << "%" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 1;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double freetotal = statex.ullAvailPageFile / 1024 / 1024;
		freetotal = freetotal / 1024;
		cout << "æ€»ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << freetotal <<" GB" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 2;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double freevir = (totalvir - freetotal) - (totalphy * statex.dwMemoryLoad / 100.0);
		cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨é‡ï¼š" << setprecision(3) << freevir <<" GB" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 3;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double usevir = freevir * 100 / (totalvir - totalphy);
		cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š";
		printf("%.2f%%", usevir);
		cout << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 4;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "CPUåˆ©ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << right << setprecision(2) << setw(6) << cpu << "%" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 5;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "CPUç©ºé—²ç‡ï¼š    " << setw(6) << cpuidle << "%"<<endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 6;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "-------------------------------------------------------" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 7;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "æŒ‰ä»»æ„é”®é€€å‡ºç¨‹åº" << endl;
		preidleTime = idleTime;
		prekernelTime = kernelTime;
		preuserTime = userTime;
	}
	cout << endl;
	
}

#include <direct.h>
void getFiles(string path, string path2, vector<string>& files)
{
	//æ–‡ä»¶å¥æŸ„  
	long   hFile = 0;
	//æ–‡ä»¶ä¿¡æ¯  
	struct _finddata_t fileinfo;
	string p, p2;
	if ((hFile = _findfirst(p.assign(path).append(path2).append("\\*").c_str(), &fileinfo)) != -1)// _findfirst(p.assign(path).append(path2).append("\\*").c_str(), &fileinfo)) != -1
	{
		do
		{
			//å¦‚æœæ˜¯ç›®å½•,è¿­ä»£ä¹‹  
			//å¦‚æœä¸æ˜¯,åŠ å…¥åˆ—è¡¨  
			if ((fileinfo.attrib & _A_SUBDIR))
			{
				if (strcmp(fileinfo.name, ".") != 0 && strcmp(fileinfo.name, "..") != 0)
				{
					getFiles(p.assign(path).append("\\"), p2.assign(fileinfo.name).append("\\"), files);
				}
			}
			else
			{
				files.push_back(p.assign(path2).append(fileinfo.name));  //è¿™ä¸€è¡Œå¯ä»¥ç»™å‡ºç›¸å¯¹è·¯å¾„
				//files.push_back(p.assign(fileinfo.name) );  //è¿™ä¸€è¡Œå¯ä»¥ç»™å‡ºæ–‡ä»¶å 
			}
		} while (_findnext(hFile, &fileinfo) == 0);
		_findclose(hFile);
	}
}


void getFilesAll(string path, vector<string>& files)
{
	//æ–‡ä»¶å¥æŸ„
	long hFile = 0;
	//æ–‡ä»¶ä¿¡æ¯
	struct _finddata_t fileinfo;
	string p;
	if ((hFile = _findfirst(p.assign(path).append("\\*").c_str(), &fileinfo)) != -1)
	{
		do
		{
			if ((fileinfo.attrib & _A_SUBDIR))
			{
				if (strcmp(fileinfo.name, ".") != 0 && strcmp(fileinfo.name, "..") != 0)
				{
					//files.push_back(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name));
					getFilesAll(p.assign(path).append("\\\\").append(fileinfo.name), files);
				}
			}
			else
			{
				files.push_back(p.assign(path).append("\\\\").append(fileinfo.name));
			}
		} while (_findnext(hFile, &fileinfo) == 0);
		_findclose(hFile);
	}
}

void getJustCurrentFile(string path, vector<string>& files)
{
	//æ–‡ä»¶å¥æŸ„ 
	long  hFile = 0;
	//æ–‡ä»¶ä¿¡æ¯ 
	struct _finddata_t fileinfo;
	string p;
	if ((hFile = _findfirst(p.assign(path).append("\\*").c_str(), &fileinfo)) != -1)
	{
		do
		{
			if ((fileinfo.attrib & _A_SUBDIR))
			{
				;
			}
			else
			{
				files.push_back(fileinfo.name);
				//files.push_back(p.assign(path).append("\\").append(fileinfo.name) ); 
			}
		} while (_findnext(hFile, &fileinfo) == 0);
		_findclose(hFile);
	}
}

string solve(string& s1, string& s2)
{
	if (s2.size() == 0)
		return s1;
	for (int i = 0;i < (int)(s1.size() - s2.size() + 1);)
	{
		if (s1.substr(i, s2.size()) == s2)
		{
			s1.erase(i, s2.size());
		}
		else
			i++;
	}
	return s1;
}


BOOL SetConsoleColor(WORD wAttributes)
{
	HANDLE hConsole = GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE);
	if (hConsole == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE)
		return FALSE;
	return SetConsoleTextAttribute(hConsole, wAttributes);
}

#define FOREGROUND_BLUE      0x0001 // text color contains blue.æ–‡æœ¬é¢œè‰²åŒ…å«è“è‰²ã€‚
#define FOREGROUND_GREEN     0x0002 // text color contains green.
#define FOREGROUND_RED       0x0004 // text color contains red.
#define FOREGROUND_INTENSITY 0x0008 // text color is intensified.æ–‡æœ¬é¢œè‰²å¢å¼ºã€‚
#define BACKGROUND_BLUE      0x0010 // background color contains blue.//èƒŒæ™¯è‰²åŒ…å«è“è‰²ã€‚
#define BACKGROUND_GREEN     0x0020 // background color contains green.
#define BACKGROUND_RED       0x0040 // background color contains red.
#define BACKGROUND_INTENSITY 0x0080 // background color is intensified.
#define COMMON_LVB_LEADING_BYTE    0x0100 // Leading Byte of DBCS
#define COMMON_LVB_TRAILING_BYTE   0x0200 // Trailing Byte of DBCS
#define COMMON_LVB_GRID_HORIZONTAL 0x0400 // DBCS: Grid attribute: top horizontal.
#define COMMON_LVB_GRID_LVERTICAL  0x0800 // DBCS: Grid attribute: left vertical.
#define COMMON_LVB_GRID_RVERTICAL  0x1000 // DBCS: Grid attribute: right vertical.
#define COMMON_LVB_REVERSE_VIDEO   0x4000 // DBCS: Reverse fore/back ground attribute.
#define COMMON_LVB_UNDERSCORE      0x8000 // DBCS: Underscore.
#define COMMON_LVB_SBCSDBCS        0x0300 // SBCS or DBCS flag.

	finalout << setw(jianju) << "æœ‰æ•ˆå­—ç¬¦æ€»æ•°ï¼š" << strtotal << endl;
	finalout << setw(jianju) << "ç©ºæ ¼æ•°ï¼š" << strspace << endl;
	finalout << setw(jianju) << "è¡Œæ•°ï¼š" << str13 << endl;
	finalout << endl;
	finalout.close();
	cout << "æœ€ç»ˆç»“æœä¿å­˜åœ¨ç›¸å¯¹è·¯å¾„ä¸‹" << endl;
	delete[]paths;


	//*************************è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ***************************************
	runend();

	system("pause");

	



	rundisplay();                                                                   //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æœæ˜¾ç¤º
	_getch();
	//closegraph();
	// system("pause");
	//Sleep(10000);
	return 0;
}

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šä½è¿ç®—ç¬¦
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š å¤åˆä½èµ‹å€¼è¿ç®—ç¬¦
 * <p>
 * è¿ç®—ç¬¦	 å«ä¹‰	     å®ä¾‹	        ç»“æœ
 * &=	æŒ‰ä½ä¸èµ‹å€¼	num1 &= num2    ç­‰ä»·äº num 1=num 1 & num2
 * |=	æŒ‰ä½æˆ–èµ‹å€¼	num1 |= num2	ç­‰ä»·äº num 1=num 1 | num2
 * ^=	æŒ‰ä½å¼‚æˆ–èµ‹å€¼	num1 ^= num2	ç­‰ä»·äº num 1=num 1 ^ num2
 * -=	æŒ‰ä½å–åèµ‹å€¼	num1 ~= num2	ç­‰ä»·äº num 1=num 1 ~ num2
 * Â«=	æŒ‰ä½å·¦ç§»èµ‹å€¼	num1 Â«= num2	ç­‰ä»·äº num 1=num 1 Â« num2
 * Â»=	æŒ‰ä½å³ç§»èµ‹å€¼	num1 Â»= num2	ç­‰ä»·äº num 1=num 1 Â» num2
 * <p>
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/9/20
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 19:23
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 */

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        int a = 1;
        int b = 2;
        int c = 3;
        a &= 4;
        a |= 4;
        a ^= c;
        a -= 6;
        b >>= 1;
        c <<= 1;
        System.out.println("a = " + a);
        System.out.println("b = " + b);
        System.out.println("c = " + c);
    }
}

        {
            double final_runtime;

            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "å¾®ç§’");
        }
        else if ((endTime - startTime) >= 1000000 && (endTime - startTime) < 10000000000L)
        {

            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 1000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "æ¯«ç§’");
        }
        else
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 10000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 100000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "ç§’");
        }
        //------------------------------------------------------
        // ç»™pä¸­çš„å±æ€§èµ‹å€¼

{

    private int age;

    {
        return name;
    }

    {
        this.name = name;

    {
        return age;
    }

    {
        this.age = age;
    }

    public void talk()
    {
        StringBuilder s=new StringBuilder();
        s.append("æˆ‘æ˜¯ï¼š").append(name).append("ï¼Œä»Šå¹´ï¼š").append(age).append("å²");
        System.out.println(s);

    protected int age;

    /********* end *********/

                .append("ï¼ŒèŒä¸šï¼š").append(this.occupation).append("ï¼");
        System.out.println(s);
    }

    /********* end *********/
}

        // é€šè¿‡æœ‰å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°å®ä¾‹åŒ–Dogç±»å¯¹è±¡dog
        // dogè°ƒç”¨talk()æ–¹æ³•
        // dogè°ƒç”¨eat()æ–¹æ³•

        dog.eat();

        // é€šè¿‡æœ‰å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°å®ä¾‹åŒ–Catç±»å¯¹è±¡cat
        // catè°ƒç”¨talk()æ–¹æ³•
        // catè°ƒç”¨eat()æ–¹æ³•
        /********* begin *********/
        Cat cat = new Cat(catName, catSex, catWeight);
        cat.talk();
        cat.eat();

    }

// æŠ½è±¡ç±»Pet å°è£…å±æ€§nameå’Œsex
// æ„é€ å‡½æ•°åˆå§‹åŒ–nameå’Œsex
// å£°æ˜æŠ½è±¡æ–¹æ³•talk()
// å£°æ˜æŠ½è±¡æ–¹æ³•eat()
abstract class Pet
{
    /********* begin *********/
    protected String name;
    protected String sex;

    abstract void talk();

    abstract void eat();
    /********* end *********/
}

// Dogç±»ç»§æ‰¿è‡ªPetç±» å°è£…å±æ€§color
// æ„é€ å‡½æ•°åˆå§‹åŒ–nameã€sexå’Œcolor
// å®ç°è‡ªå·±çš„talk()æ–¹æ³•å’Œeat()æ–¹æ³•
// talk()è¾“å‡º'åç§°ï¼šnameï¼Œæ€§åˆ«ï¼šsexï¼Œé¢œè‰²ï¼šcolorï¼Œæ±ªæ±ªå«'
// eat()è¾“å‡º'nameåƒéª¨å¤´'
class Dog extends Pet
{
    /********* begin *********/
    private final String color;

    Dog(String name, String sex, String color)
    {
        this.name = name;
        this.sex = sex;
        this.color = color;
    }


    @Override
    void talk()
    {
        System.out.println("åç§°ï¼š" + this.name + "ï¼Œæ€§åˆ«ï¼š" + this.sex + "ï¼Œé¢œè‰²ï¼š" + this.color + "ï¼Œæ±ªæ±ªå«");
    }

    @Override
    void eat()
    {
        System.out.println(this.name + "åƒéª¨å¤´ï¼");
    }
    /********* end *********/
}

// Catç±»ç»§æ‰¿è‡ªPetç±» å°è£…å±æ€§weight
// æ„é€ å‡½æ•°åˆå§‹åŒ–nameã€sexå’Œweight
// å®ç°è‡ªå·±çš„talk()æ–¹æ³•å’Œeat()æ–¹æ³•
// talk()è¾“å‡º'åç§°ï¼šnameï¼Œæ€§åˆ«ï¼šsexï¼Œä½“é‡ï¼šweight kgï¼Œå–µå–µå«'
// eat()è¾“å‡º'nameåƒé±¼'
class Cat extends Pet
{
    /********* begin *********/
    private final double weight;

    Cat(String name, String sex, double weight)
    {
        this.name = name;
        this.sex = sex;
        this.weight = weight;
    }

    @Override
    void talk()
    {
        System.out.println("åç§°ï¼š" + this.name + "ï¼Œæ€§åˆ«ï¼š" + this.sex + "ï¼Œä½“é‡ï¼š" + this.weight + "kgï¼Œå–µå–µå«");
    }

    @Override
    void eat()
    {
        System.out.println(this.name + "åƒé±¼ï¼");
    }

    /********* end *********/

interface SpeakEnglish
{
    /********* begin *********/
    abstract void speak();
    /********* end *********/
}

// å®šä¹‰äººçš„æŠ½è±¡ç±»Person å°è£…nameå’Œage
// æ— å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°
// æœ‰å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°åˆå§‹åŒ–nameå’Œage
// å®šä¹‰å…·ä½“æ–¹æ³•sleep() è¾“å‡º'äººéƒ½æ˜¯è¦ç¡è§‰çš„'
// æŠ½è±¡æ–¹æ³•eat()ï¼ˆåƒçš„ä¸ä¸€æ ·ï¼‰
abstract class Person
{
    /********* begin *********/
    protected String name;
    protected int age;

    public void sleep()
    {
        System.out.println("äººéƒ½æ˜¯è¦ç¡è§‰çš„");
    }

    public abstract void eat();
    /********* end *********/
}

// å®šä¹‰è¿åŠ¨å‘˜Playerï¼ˆæŠ½è±¡ç±»ï¼‰ç»§æ‰¿è‡ªPersonç±»

abstract class Player extends Person
{
    /********* begin *********/
    public Player()
    {

    }

    public Player(String name, int age)
    {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    public abstract void study();
    /********* end *********/
}

abstract class Coach extends Person

    }

    /********* end *********/
}

        float memory;
        memory = r.totalMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf("JVMæ€»å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);
        memory = r.freeMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf(" ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);
        memory = r.totalMemory() - r.freeMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf("å·²ä½¿ç”¨çš„å†…å­˜ï¼š%.4fMB\n", memory);

    }

import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šå†’æ³¡æ’åºæ³•
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/9/26
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 20:13
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 */

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        Scanner scan = new Scanner(System.in);
        double[] score = new double[5];
        for (int i = 0; i < score.length; i++)
        {
            System.out.print("è¯·è¾“å…¥ç¬¬ " + (i + 1) + " ä¸ªæˆç»©ï¼š");
            score[i] = scan.nextDouble();
        }
        System.out.println("æ’åºå‰çš„å…ƒç´ å€¼ï¼š");
        for (double val : score)
        {
            System.out.print(val + "\t");
        }
        System.out.println();

        System.out.println("é€šè¿‡å†’æ³¡æ’åºæ–¹æ³•å¯¹æ•°ç»„è¿›è¡Œæ’åºï¼š");
        for (int i = 0; i < score.length - 1; i++)
        {
            // æ¯”è¾ƒç›¸é‚»ä¸¤ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ï¼Œè¾ƒå¤§çš„æ•°å¾€åå†’æ³¡
            for (int j = 0; j < score.length - 1 - i; j++)
            {
                if (score[j] > score[j + 1])
                {
                    double temp = score[j + 1]; // æŠŠç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ å€¼ä¿å­˜åˆ°ä¸´æ—¶å˜é‡ä¸­
                    score[j + 1] = score[j]; // æŠŠç¬¬äºŒä¸ªå…ƒç´ å€¼è½¬ç§»åˆ°ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ å˜é‡ä¸­
                    score[j] = temp; // æŠŠä¸´æ—¶å˜é‡ï¼ˆç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ çš„åŸå€¼ï¼‰ä¿å­˜åˆ°ç¬¬äºŒä¸ªå…ƒç´ ä¸­
                }
                System.out.print(score[j] + " "); // å¯¹æ’åºåçš„æ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ è¿›è¡Œè¾“å‡º
            }
            System.out.print("ã€");
            for (int j = score.length - 1 - i; j < score.length; j++)
            {
                System.out.print(score[j] + " ");
            }
            System.out.println("ã€‘");
        }
    }
}

        this.age = age;

        this.Name = "name";
        this.age = 0;

        // ä½¿ç”¨newå…³é”®å­—åˆ›å»ºå¯¹è±¡

        System.out.println(student1);

        // è°ƒç”¨ java.lang.Class çš„ newInstance() æ–¹æ³•åˆ›å»ºå¯¹è±¡
        Class c1 = Class.forName("Student");
        Student student2 = (Student) c1.newInstance();
        System.out.println(student2);
        System.out.println("-------------------è°ƒç”¨å¯¹è±¡çš„ clone() æ–¹æ³•åˆ›å»ºå¯¹è±¡----------");
        // è°ƒç”¨å¯¹è±¡çš„ clone() æ–¹æ³•åˆ›å»ºå¯¹è±¡
        Student student3 = (Student) student2.clone();
        System.out.println(student3);
    }

        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥æœˆä»½:");
        int month = sc.nextInt();
        boolean isRen;
        if ((year % 4 == 0 && year % 100 != 0) || (year % 400 == 0))
        {
            System.out.println(year + "é—°å¹´");
            isRen = true;
        }
        else
        {
            System.out.println(year + "å¹³å¹´");
            isRen = false;
        }
        int day;
        switch (month)
        {
            case 1:
            case 3:
            case 5:
            case 7:
            case 8:
            case 10:
            case 12:
                day = 31;
                break;
            case 4:
            case 6:
            case 9:
            case 11:
                day = 30;
                break;
            default:
                if (isRen)
                {
                    day = 29;
                }
                else
                {
                    day = 28;
                }
                break;
        }
        System.out.println(year + "å¹´" + month + "æœˆå…±æœ‰" + day + "å¤©");
    }

package com.stu;

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šåŒ…
 * Package(åŒ…å): com.stu
 * Class(ç±»å): Student
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/10/7
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 19:39
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 */

public class Student
{
    private String name;
    private int age;
    private String sex;
    private long StudentID;

    public Student(String name, int age, String sex, long studentID)
    {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.sex = sex;
        StudentID = studentID;
    }

    public String getName()
    {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name)
    {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getAge()
    {
        return age;
    }

    public void setAge(int age)
    {
        this.age = age;
    }

    public String getSex()
    {
        return sex;
    }

    public void setSex(String sex)
    {
        this.sex = sex;
    }

    public long getStudentID()
    {
        return StudentID;
    }

    public void setStudentID(long studentID)
    {
        StudentID = studentID;
    }

    public StringBuilder display()
    {
        StringBuilder s;
        s = new StringBuilder();
        s.append("å§“åï¼š").append(getName());
        s.append("\nå¹´é¾„:").append(getAge());
        s.append("\næ€§åˆ«ï¼š").append(getSex());
        s.append("\nå­¦å·:").append(getStudentID());
        return s;
    }
}

LARGE_INTEGER time_start;	                                //å¼€å§‹æ—¶é—´
LARGE_INTEGER time_over;	                                //ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
double dqFreq;		                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡
LARGE_INTEGER f;	                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡

inline void runstart()
{
	QueryPerformanceFrequency(&f);
	dqFreq = (double)f.QuadPart;
	t1 = __rdtsc();
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_start);	       //è®¡æ—¶å¼€å§‹
}
inline void runend()
{
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_over);	        //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ
	run_time = 1000 * (time_over.QuadPart - time_start.QuadPart) / dqFreq;
	t2 = __rdtsc();
	t3 = t2 - t1;
}
void ShowProcessMemoryUsageInfo()
{
	HANDLE handle = GetCurrentProcess();
	PROCESS_MEMORY_COUNTERS pmc;
	GetProcessMemoryInfo(handle, &pmc, sizeof(pmc));
	float memoryUsage_M = pmc.WorkingSetSize / (1024.0 * 1024.0);
	float memoryUsage_K = pmc.WorkingSetSize / 1024.0;
	std::cout << std::fixed << setprecision(0) << "ç¨‹åºå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << memoryUsage_K << " KB = " << setprecision(2) << memoryUsage_M << " MB" << std::endl;
}
__int64 CompareFileTime(FILETIME time1, FILETIME time2)//è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•´æ•°æ—¶é—´
{
	__int64 a = static_cast<long long>(time1.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time1.dwLowDateTime;
	__int64 b = static_cast<long long>(time2.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time2.dwLowDateTime;
	return   (b - a);
}

	cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨é‡ï¼š" << setprecision(3) << freevir << " GB" << endl;

	cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š";
	printf("%.2f%%", usevir);
	cout << endl;
	cout << "CPUåˆ©ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << right << setprecision(2) << setw(6) << 0.00 << "%" << endl;
	cout << "CPUç©ºé—²ç‡ï¼š    " << setw(6) << 100.0<< "%" << endl;
	cout << "-------------------------------------------------------" << endl;
	cout << "æŒ‰ä»»æ„é”®é€€å‡ºç¨‹åº" << endl;
	while (!_kbhit())
	{
		GlobalMemoryStatusEx(&statex);
		WaitForSingleObject(hEvent, 1000);
		res = GetSystemTimes(&idleTime, &kernelTime, &userTime);
		int idle = CompareFileTime(preidleTime, idleTime);
		int kernel = CompareFileTime(prekernelTime, kernelTime);
		int user = CompareFileTime(preuserTime, userTime);
		float cpu = (kernel + user - idle) * 100.0 / (kernel + user);
		float cpuidle = (idle) * 100.0 / (kernel + user);
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 0;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		//cout << "å†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << statex.dwMemoryLoad << "%" << endl;
		double freephy = statex.ullAvailPhys / 1024 / 1024;
		freephy = freephy / 1024;
		double usephy = (totalphy - freephy) * 100.0 / totalphy;
		cout << "å†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << usephy << "%" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 1;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double freetotal = statex.ullAvailPageFile / 1024 / 1024;
		freetotal = freetotal / 1024;
		cout << "æ€»ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << freetotal <<" GB" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 2;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double freevir = (totalvir - freetotal) - (totalphy * statex.dwMemoryLoad / 100.0);
		cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨é‡ï¼š" << setprecision(3) << freevir <<" GB" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 3;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double usevir = freevir * 100 / (totalvir - totalphy);
		cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š";
		printf("%.2f%%", usevir);
		cout << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 4;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "CPUåˆ©ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << right << setprecision(2) << setw(6) << cpu << "%" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 5;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "CPUç©ºé—²ç‡ï¼š    " << setw(6) << cpuidle << "%"<<endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 6;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "-------------------------------------------------------" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 7;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "æŒ‰ä»»æ„é”®é€€å‡ºç¨‹åº" << endl;
		preidleTime = idleTime;
		prekernelTime = kernelTime;
		preuserTime = userTime;
	}
	cout << endl;
	
}

public class Employee
{
    private String name;
    private double salary;

    Employee()
    {
        name = "unknown";
        salary = 0.0;
    }

    Employee(String name, double salary)
    {
        this.name = name;
        this.salary = salary;
    }

    public String getName()
    {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name)
    {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public double getSalary()
    {
        return salary;
    }

    public void setSalary(double salary)
    {
        this.salary = salary;
    }
}

                                                                        //ä½œè€…QQ1296193245
using namespace std;
#pragma warning(disable : 4996)
#pragma comment (lib,"ddraw.lib")
#pragma comment(lib,"sapi.lib")
#pragma comment(lib,"ole32.lib")
#pragma comment(lib,"Winmm.lib")                     // å¼•ç”¨ Windows Multimedia API
#pragma intrinsic(__rdtsc)
unsigned __int64 t1, t2, t3, t4;
double run_time;                                                   //å¾®ç§’çº§ç®—æ³•æ—¶é—´è®¡æ—¶å™¨
LARGE_INTEGER time_start;	                                //å¼€å§‹æ—¶é—´
LARGE_INTEGER time_over;	                                //ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
double dqFreq;		                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡
LARGE_INTEGER f;	                                               //è®¡æ—¶å™¨é¢‘ç‡
double tt;
long double totaltime;

inline void runstart()
{
	QueryPerformanceFrequency(&f);
	dqFreq = (double)f.QuadPart;
	t1 = __rdtsc();
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_start);	       //è®¡æ—¶å¼€å§‹
}
inline void runend()
{
	QueryPerformanceCounter(&time_over);	        //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ
	run_time = 1000 * (time_over.QuadPart - time_start.QuadPart) / dqFreq;
	t2 = __rdtsc();
	t3 = t2 - t1;
}
void ShowProcessMemoryUsageInfo()
{
	HANDLE handle = GetCurrentProcess();
	PROCESS_MEMORY_COUNTERS pmc;
	GetProcessMemoryInfo(handle, &pmc, sizeof(pmc));
	float memoryUsage_M = pmc.WorkingSetSize / (1024.0 * 1024.0);
	float memoryUsage_K = pmc.WorkingSetSize / 1024.0;
	std::cout << std::fixed << setprecision(0) << "ç¨‹åºå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << memoryUsage_K << " KB = " << setprecision(2) << memoryUsage_M << " MB" << std::endl;
}
__int64 CompareFileTime(FILETIME time1, FILETIME time2)//è½¬æ¢ä¸ºæ•´æ•°æ—¶é—´
{
	__int64 a = static_cast<long long>(time1.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time1.dwLowDateTime;
	__int64 b = static_cast<long long>(time2.dwHighDateTime) << 32 | time2.dwLowDateTime;
	return   (b - a);
}
void rundisplay()
{
	cout << endl;

	if (t3 < 10000)
	{
		cout << "CPUè„‰å†²æ•°ï¼š" << (t3) << endl;
	}
	else if (t3 < 100000000 && t3 >= 10000)
	{
		tt = t3;
		cout << "CPUè„‰å†²æ•°ï¼š" << (tt) / 10000 << "ä¸‡" << endl;
	}
	else if (t3 > 100000000000)
	{
		t4 = t3;
		t4 = t3 / 10000000;
		tt = t4;
		cout << "CPUè„‰å†²æ•°ï¼š" << (tt) / 10 << "äº¿" << endl;
	}
	else
	{
		t4 = t3;
		t4 = t3 / 10000;
		tt = t4;
		cout << "CPUè„‰å†²æ•°ï¼š" << (tt) / 10000 << "äº¿" << endl;
	}
	if (run_time > 10000)
	{
		cout << "ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š" << run_time / 1000 << "ç§’" << endl;
	}
	else if (run_time < 1)
	{
		cout << "ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š" << run_time * 1000 << "å¾®ç§’" << endl;
	}
	else
	{
		cout << "ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š" << run_time << "æ¯«ç§’" << endl;
	}
	totaltime = clock();
	cout << "ç¨‹åºè¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š" << totaltime / 1000 << "ç§’" << endl;
	if (run_time > 0.4)
	{
		double frequency = t3 / run_time / 1000;
		cout << "CPUé¢‘ç‡ï¼š" << frequency << "MHZ" << endl;
	}
	ShowProcessMemoryUsageInfo();
	long lRet;
	HKEY hKey;
	TCHAR tchData[64];
	DWORD dwSize;
	lRet = RegOpenKeyEx(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, L"Hardware\\Description\\System\\CentralProcessor\\0", 0, KEY_QUERY_VALUE, &hKey);
	if (lRet == ERROR_SUCCESS)
	{
		dwSize = sizeof(tchData);
		lRet = RegQueryValueEx(hKey, L"ProcessorNameString", NULL, NULL, (LPBYTE)tchData, &dwSize);
		if (lRet == ERROR_SUCCESS)
		{
			cout << "CPU åå­—ï¼š";
			wcout << tchData << endl;
		}
		else
		{
			cout << "CPU åå­—ï¼š";

		}
	}
	else
	{
		cout << "CPU åå­—ï¼š";
		wcout << L"æœªçŸ¥" << endl;
	}
	RegCloseKey(hKey);
	MEMORYSTATUSEX statex;
	statex.dwLength = sizeof(statex);
	GlobalMemoryStatusEx(&statex);
	double totalphy = statex.ullTotalPhys / 1024 / 1024;
	totalphy = totalphy / 1024;
	cout << "æ€»ç‰©ç†å†…å­˜ï¼š    " << setprecision(4) << left << setw(7) << totalphy << " GB" << endl;
	double totalvir = statex.ullTotalPageFile / 1024 / 1024;
	totalvir = totalvir / 1024;
	cout << "æ€»è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ï¼š    " << setw(7) << totalvir - totalphy << " GB" << endl;
	HANDLE hConsole = GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE);
	COORD coordScreen = { 0, 0 }; //å…‰æ ‡ä½ç½®
	CONSOLE_SCREEN_BUFFER_INFO csbi{};
	if (GetConsoleScreenBufferInfo(hConsole, &csbi))
	{
		//printf("å…‰æ ‡åæ ‡:(%d,%d)\n", csbi.dwCursorPosition.X, csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y);
	}
	HANDLE   hStdout;
	//   å…‰æ ‡ä½ç½®   
	COORD     cursorPos;
	//   æ ‡å‡†è¾“å‡ºå¥æŸ„   
	hStdout = GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE);
	HANDLE hEvent;
	BOOL res;
	FILETIME preidleTime;
	FILETIME prekernelTime;
	FILETIME preuserTime;
	FILETIME idleTime;
	FILETIME kernelTime;
	FILETIME userTime;
	res = GetSystemTimes(&idleTime, &kernelTime, &userTime);
	preidleTime = idleTime;
	prekernelTime = kernelTime;
	preuserTime = userTime;
	hEvent = CreateEvent(NULL, FALSE, FALSE, NULL);// åˆå§‹å€¼ä¸º nonsignaled ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æ¯æ¬¡è§¦å‘åè‡ªåŠ¨è®¾ç½®ä¸ºnonsignaled
	double freephy = statex.ullAvailPhys / 1024 / 1024;
	freephy = freephy / 1024;
	double usephy = (totalphy - freephy) * 100.0 / totalphy;
	cout << "å†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << usephy << "%" << endl;
	double freetotal = statex.ullAvailPageFile / 1024 / 1024;
	freetotal = freetotal / 1024;
	cout << "æ€»ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << freetotal << " GB" << endl;
	double freevir = (totalvir - freetotal) - (totalphy * statex.dwMemoryLoad / 100.0);
	cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨é‡ï¼š" << setprecision(3) << freevir << " GB" << endl;
	double usevir = freevir * 100 / (totalvir - totalphy);
	cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š";
	printf("%.2f%%", usevir);
	cout << endl;
	cout << "CPUåˆ©ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << right << setprecision(2) << setw(6) << 0.00 << "%" << endl;
	cout << "CPUç©ºé—²ç‡ï¼š    " << setw(6) << 100.0<< "%" << endl;
	cout << "-------------------------------------------------------" << endl;
	cout << "æŒ‰ä»»æ„é”®é€€å‡ºç¨‹åº" << endl;
	while (!_kbhit())
	{
		GlobalMemoryStatusEx(&statex);
		WaitForSingleObject(hEvent, 1000);
		res = GetSystemTimes(&idleTime, &kernelTime, &userTime);
		int idle = CompareFileTime(preidleTime, idleTime);
		int kernel = CompareFileTime(prekernelTime, kernelTime);
		int user = CompareFileTime(preuserTime, userTime);
		float cpu = (kernel + user - idle) * 100.0 / (kernel + user);
		float cpuidle = (idle) * 100.0 / (kernel + user);
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 0;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		//cout << "å†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š" << statex.dwMemoryLoad << "%" << endl;
		double freephy = statex.ullAvailPhys / 1024 / 1024;
		freephy = freephy / 1024;
		double usephy = (totalphy - freephy) * 100.0 / totalphy;
		cout << "å†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << usephy << "%" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 1;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double freetotal = statex.ullAvailPageFile / 1024 / 1024;
		freetotal = freetotal / 1024;
		cout << "æ€»ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š    " << setprecision(3) << freetotal <<" GB" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 2;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double freevir = (totalvir - freetotal) - (totalphy * statex.dwMemoryLoad / 100.0);
		cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨é‡ï¼š" << setprecision(3) << freevir <<" GB" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 3;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		double usevir = freevir * 100 / (totalvir - totalphy);
		cout << "è™šæ‹Ÿå†…å­˜ä½¿ç”¨ç‡ï¼š";
		printf("%.2f%%", usevir);
		cout << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 4;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "CPUåˆ©ç”¨ç‡ï¼š    " << right << setprecision(2) << setw(6) << cpu << "%" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 5;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "CPUç©ºé—²ç‡ï¼š    " << setw(6) << cpuidle << "%"<<endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 6;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "-------------------------------------------------------" << endl;
		cursorPos.X = 0;
		cursorPos.Y = csbi.dwCursorPosition.Y + 7;
		SetConsoleCursorPosition(hStdout, cursorPos);
		cout << "æŒ‰ä»»æ„é”®é€€å‡ºç¨‹åº" << endl;

		prekernelTime = kernelTime;
		preuserTime = userTime;
	}

int main()
{

	//*************************************************************************



	//*************************************************************************
	runstart();
	//*************************è®¡æ—¶å¼€å§‹***************************************
	int strtotal = 0;
	int str13 = 0;
	ofstream fileout("out.txt", ios::out);
	ifstream file("main.cpp", ios::in);
		if (!file)
		{
			cout << "æ–‡ä»¶æ‰“å¼€å¤±è´¥";
		}
		char c;
		while (!file.eof())
		{
			c=file.get();
			//cout << c;
			fileout << c;
			if (c == '\n')
			{
				str13++;
			}
			else
			{
				strtotal++;
			}
		}
		file.close();
		fileout.close();
		cout << "å­—ç¬¦æ€»æ•°ï¼š" << strtotal << endl;
		cout << "è¡Œæ•°ï¼š" << str13 << endl;

	//*************************è®¡æ—¶ç»“æŸ***************************************
	runend();



	



	rundisplay();                                                                   //è®¡æ—¶ç»“æœæ˜¾ç¤º
	_getch();
	//closegraph();
	// system("pause");
	//Sleep(10000);
	return 0;
}

public class Figure
{
    double dim1;
    double dim2;

    Figure(double d1, double d2)
    {
        // æœ‰å‚çš„æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•
        this.dim1 = d1;
        this.dim2 = d2;
    }

    double area()
    {
        // ç”¨äºè®¡ç®—å¯¹è±¡çš„é¢ç§¯
        System.out.println("çˆ¶ç±»ä¸­è®¡ç®—å¯¹è±¡é¢ç§¯çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ²¡æœ‰å®é™…æ„ä¹‰ï¼Œéœ€è¦åœ¨å­ç±»ä¸­é‡å†™ã€‚");
        return 0;
    }
}

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šå¤šæ€
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Class(ç±»å): Rectangle
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/10/11
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 22:16
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 */

public class Rectangle extends Figure
{

    Rectangle(double d1, double d2)
    {
        super(d1, d2);
    }

    double area()
    {
        System.out.println("ä¸‰è§’å½¢çš„é¢ç§¯ï¼š");
        return super.dim1 * super.dim2 / 2;
    }
}

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šå¤šæ€
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Class(ç±»å): square
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/10/11
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 22:18
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 */

public class square extends Figure
{

    square(double d1, double d2)
    {
        super(d1, d2);
    }

    double area()
    {
        if (super.dim1 == super.dim2)
        {
            System.out.println("æ­£æ–¹å½¢çš„é¢ç§¯ï¼š");
            return super.dim1 * 4;
        }
        else
        {
            System.out.println("é”™è¯¯ï¼ï¼");
            return 0.0;
        }
    }
}

        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime);
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "å¾®ç§’");
        }
        else if ((endTime - startTime) >= 1000000 && (endTime - startTime) < 10000000000L)
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 1000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "æ¯«ç§’");
        }
        else
        {
            double final_runtime;

            final_runtime = final_runtime / 100000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "ç§’");
        }

        float memory;

        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf("JVMæ€»å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);
        memory = r.freeMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf(" ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);
        memory = r.totalMemory() - r.freeMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf("å·²ä½¿ç”¨çš„å†…å­˜ï¼š%.4fMB\n", memory);

    }

import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šå¤šæ¡ä»¶ if-else-if è¯­å¥
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š å‡è®¾æŸå­¦æ ¡å¯¹æˆç»©çš„åˆ¤æ–­æ ‡å‡†æ˜¯ï¼šä¸ä½äº 90ï¼Œå¯ä»¥è¯„ä¸ºä¼˜ç§€ï¼›
 * ä½äº 90 ä½†ä¸ä½äº 80ï¼Œå¯ä»¥è¯„ä¸ºè‰¯å¥½ï¼›ä½äº 80 ä½†ä¸ä½äº 60ï¼Œå¯ä»¥è¯„ä¸ºä¸­ç­‰ï¼›å¦åˆ™è¯„ä¸ºå·®ã€‚

 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 20:54
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 */

public class test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        System.out.printf("è¯·è¾“å…¥æˆç»©ï¼š");
        Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
        int score = input.nextInt();
        if (score >= 90)
        {
            System.out.println("ä¼˜ç§€");
        }
        else if (score >= 80)
        {
            System.out.println("è‰¯å¥½");
        }
        else if (score >= 60)
        {
            System.out.println("ä¸­ç­‰");
        }
        else
        {
            System.out.println("å·®");
        }
    }
}

import java.util.Objects;

/*
åœ¨ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡è¿›å…¥ç³»ç»Ÿæ—¶è¦æ±‚ç®¡ç†å‘˜è®¾ç½®ä¸€ä¸ªå¯†ç ï¼Œå‡ºäºå®‰å…¨è€ƒè™‘å¯†ç éœ€è¦è¾“å…¥ä¸¤æ¬¡ï¼Œ
å¦‚æœä¸¤æ¬¡è¾“å…¥çš„å¯†ç ä¸€è‡´æ‰ç”Ÿæ•ˆï¼Œå¦åˆ™æç¤ºå¤±è´¥ã€‚å…·ä½“å®ç°ä»£ç å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š
 */
public class pass
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        String sys = "å­¦ç”Ÿä¿¡æ¯ç®¡ç†";
        System.out.println("æ¬¢è¿è¿›å…¥" + sys + "ç³»ç»Ÿ");
        System.out.println("è¯·è®¾ç½®ä¸€ä¸ªç®¡ç†å‘˜å¯†ç ï¼š");
        Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
        String pass = input.next();
        System.out.println("è¯·å†æ¬¡è¾“å…¥ï¼š");
        String pass2 = input.next();
        if (Objects.equals(pass, pass2))
        {
            System.out.println("è®¾ç½®çš„å¯†ç å·²ç»ç”Ÿæ•ˆï¼Œå¯†ç ä¸º" + pass);
        }
        else
        {
            System.out.println("ä¸¤æ¬¡è¾“å…¥çš„å¯†ç ä¸ä¸€è‡´ï¼ï¼ï¼");
        }
    }

public class test2
{

    {

        String str2 = "ABC";
        System.out.println(str1.equalsIgnoreCase(str2));    // è¾“å‡º true

        /*
        åœ¨ä¼šå‘˜ç³»ç»Ÿä¸­éœ€è¦è¾“å…¥ç”¨æˆ·åå’Œå¯†ç è¿›è¡Œæ£€éªŒï¼Œä¸‹é¢ä½¿ç”¨ equalsIgnoreCase() æ–¹æ³•å®ç°æ£€éªŒç™»å½•æ—¶ä¸åŒºåˆ†ç”¨æˆ·åå’Œå¯†ç çš„å¤§å°å†™ï¼Œ

        System.out.println("æ¬¢è¿è¿›å…¥" + sys + "ç³»ç»Ÿ");
        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥ç®¡ç†å‘˜åç§°ï¼š");
        Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
        String name = input.next(); // è·å–ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥çš„åç§°
        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥ç®¡ç†å‘˜å¯†ç ï¼š");
        input = new Scanner(System.in);
        String pass = input.next(); // è·å–ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥çš„å¯†ç 
        // æ¯”è¾ƒç”¨æˆ·åä¸å¯†ç ï¼Œæ³¨æ„æ­¤å¤„å¿½ç•¥å¤§å°å†™
        if (name.equalsIgnoreCase("admin") && pass.equalsIgnoreCase("123"))
        { // éªŒè¯
            System.out.println("ç™»å½•æˆåŠŸã€‚");
        }
        else
        {
            System.out.println("ç™»å½•å¤±è´¥ã€‚");
        }
    }

/**
 * Project name(é¡¹ç›®åç§°)ï¼šå­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„åŠ å¯†è§£å¯† encryption-and-decryption-of-strings
 * Package(åŒ…å): PACKAGE_NAME
 * Author(ä½œè€…ï¼‰: mao
 * Author QQï¼š1296193245
 * Date(åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ)ï¼š 2021/10/1
 * Time(åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´)ï¼š 19:58
 * Version(ç‰ˆæœ¬): 1.0
 * Description(æè¿°)ï¼š æ— 
 */

public class test
{
    public static String encryptAndDencrypt(String value, char secret)
    {
        byte[] bt = value.getBytes(); // å°†éœ€è¦åŠ å¯†çš„å†…å®¹è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå­—èŠ‚æ•°ç»„
        for (int i = 0; i < bt.length; i++)
        {
            if (i % 2 == 1)
            {
                bt[i] = (byte) (bt[i] ^ (5 + i + (int) secret)); // é€šè¿‡å¼‚æˆ–è¿ç®—è¿›è¡ŒåŠ å¯†
            }
            else
            {
                bt[i] = (byte) (bt[i] ^ (2 + 2 * i + (int) secret));
            }
        }
        String newresult = new String(bt, 0, bt.length); // å°†åŠ å¯†åçš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¿å­˜åˆ° newresult å˜é‡ä¸­
        return newresult;
    }

    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        Scanner scan = new Scanner(System.in);
        char secret = '1'; // åŠ å¯†æ–‡å­—ç¬¦
        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥æ‚¨æƒ³åŠ å¯†çš„å†…å®¹ï¼š");
        String pass = scan.next();
        System.out.println("åŸå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å†…å®¹ï¼š" + pass);
        String encryptResult = encryptAndDencrypt(pass, secret);
        System.out.println("åŠ å¯†åçš„å†…å®¹ï¼š" + encryptResult);
        String uncryptResult = encryptAndDencrypt(encryptResult, secret);
        System.out.println("è§£å¯†åçš„å†…å®¹ï¼š" + uncryptResult);
        System.out.println((int)'Â¿');
        System.out.println((char)191);
    }
}

public class Cat extends Animal
{

    public String str = "Catï¼šå¯çˆ±çš„å°çŒ«";
    public static String staticName = "Dogï¼šæˆ‘æ˜¯å–µæ˜Ÿäºº";

    public void eat()
    {
        System.out.println("Catï¼šåƒé¥­");
    }

    public static void staticEat()
    {
        System.out.println("Catï¼šçŒ«åœ¨åƒé¥­");
    }

    public void eatMethod()
    {
        System.out.println("Catï¼šçŒ«å–œæ¬¢åƒé±¼");
    }

    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        //------------------------------------------------------
        long startTime = System.nanoTime();   //è·å–å¼€å§‹æ—¶é—´
        //------------------------------------------------------

        Cat cat = (Cat) animal; // å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹
        System.out.println(animal.name); // è¾“å‡ºAnimalç±»çš„nameå˜é‡
        System.out.println(animal.staticName); // è¾“å‡ºAnimalç±»çš„staticNameå˜é‡
        animal.eat(); // è¾“å‡ºCatç±»çš„eat()æ–¹æ³•
        animal.staticEat(); // è¾“å‡ºAnimalç±»çš„staticEat()æ–¹æ³•
        System.out.println(cat.str); // è°ƒç”¨Catç±»çš„strå˜é‡
        cat.eatMethod(); // è°ƒç”¨Catç±»çš„eatMethod()æ–¹æ³•
        //------------------------------------------------------
        long endTime = System.nanoTime(); //è·å–ç»“æŸæ—¶é—´
        if ((endTime - startTime) < 1000000)
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime);
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "å¾®ç§’");
        }
        else if ((endTime - startTime) >= 1000000 && (endTime - startTime) < 10000000000L)
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 1000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 1000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "æ¯«ç§’");
        }
        else
        {
            double final_runtime;
            final_runtime = (endTime - startTime) / 10000;
            final_runtime = final_runtime / 100000;
            System.out.println("ç®—æ³•è¿è¡Œæ—¶é—´ï¼š " + final_runtime + "ç§’");
        }
        Runtime r = Runtime.getRuntime();
        float memory;
        memory = r.totalMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf("JVMæ€»å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);
        memory = r.freeMemory();
        memory = memory / 1024 / 1024;
        System.out.printf(" ç©ºé—²å†…å­˜ï¼š%.3fMB\n", memory);

        System.out.printf("å·²ä½¿ç”¨çš„å†…å­˜ï¼š%.4fMB\n", memory);

    }

        }

    {
        System.out.println("ä¹¦ã€Š" + this.BookName + "ã€‹çš„æ€»é¡µæ•°ä¸ºï¼š" + this.page + "é¡µ");

    {
        this.width = width;
        this.height = height;
    }

    public abstract double area();
}
